    translated: "When using a Yin attribute technique, the character enters a Yin attribute state. At this time, the character gains combat bonuses associated with the Yin attribute and some special effects: \\n1: Switching to a Yin attribute technique status, the character's attacks on those in a Soft state will receive damage multiplier bonuses.
